The location is not in an ideal location as there are lot of graffitis around the store area. The pricing is okay compared to other Indian stores. One thing which outstands this store from other Indian stores is that you do not need to go to Indian hotel/restaurant to eat Indian dishes as they cook Indian dishes and also have chairs and tables to eat inside the store.</review>

Messy and dirty just like many of the shops in India. The hot food is delicious and inexpensive and in years of eating here we have never had any issues. Great prices on produce and products but do check expiration dates. They do take debit/credit cards.</review>

< text>
Ordered from here just knowing that it's well-received, although prices were a bit on the higher side (little did we know it was vegan!). Got a mint chocolate cupcake, other chocolate cake, strawberry shortcake, and coffee cake. Coffee cake was great! All moist and amazing frosting. Shortcake was alright, but it seemed like sweet cornbread was the base. Interesting frosting too. The mint frosting was okay and the frosting skills were on point! Sometimes it was hard to tell if dairy was used. BUT the chocolate cake base was not it. It was super duper dry for both choco cake pieces. So I would go back but avoid anything chocolatey or stuff with elaborate frosting, since the actual substance wasn't high quality.</text>

<Rating>1< /Rating>< Review>
I really don't know what my problem is with this place but I have ordered twice and twice they have royally screwed up. I wish I would have never taken down my original review but they offered me a gift card in the total amount I had spent. One year later I ordered for my special needs nephew with gluten and dairy allergies. He only likes vanilla!!! vanilla cake vanilla frosting. I was very clear about this It was the only thing I cared about, Vanilla Vanilla! So I attempted an online order but couldn't since they don't take their own gift cards online. So I called over a week in advance and asked for a Sunday early afternoon delivery since that was when his bday drive-by was. They couldn't deliver it in time and we opted for Saturday since LA location flat out refused to help us. Ashley was amazing in helping us get the delivery part worked out. The cake was delivered they even threw a few little treats for the hassle and the kids loved them. Now comes Sunday, time to cut the cake and ITS CHOCOLATE!!!!!! I can not even express how disappointed I am. Their stuff is not cheap. I have spent $150 for a cake and delivery twice and I have never received the right order.  For a quick rundown the first experience I ordered a vanilla vanilla cake, white and gold trim. They sent gold and white trim no cake box (apparently they ran out) so they put it in a cardboard box that they received their coconut flour shipment in. It was too big and the cake was floating around in this box and had a bunch of thumbprints and marks from being in a gigantic box. Erin reached out and sent me a gift card for the amount I spent and I deleted the review. And now they got the cake flavor wrong. Please! be aware this is the most unorganized company I have ever dealt with.  I absolutely do not recommend this bakery.
I will say Ashley was great to work with she was super sweet, calm, and was really trying to help me. The young man who delivered the cake was also lovely. Very sweet and pleasant.</Review>

<userid>110981645693167933380<//userid>< Name>
Jennifer Allen< /Name>
<date>1479940859347<//date>< rate>
1</rate>
< Text>
Had them come to do a cleaning and safety inspection. They said our home inspector was incorrect and we didn't need the cleaning he'd recommended. So they didn't clean anything (not even the fireplace).

The safety inspection didn't take long, but ended up with the recommendation of nearly $3,500 worth of repairs (only about $2,000 were "urgent"). The sweep offered 10% if we agreed to the repairs now and just happened to have all the materials needed on his truck. I'd made arrangements to be home during the day for the appointment - my husband wasn't around. I explained I was uncomfortable making a decision about spending a couple thousand dollars without talking to him. The sweep asked me to call him. I said I'd rather talk to him. He really, really wanted me to make a decision today - even offered 15% off if I did (after spending 15 minutes or so out in his truck talking to the boss after I told him I wasn't going to commit to spending that kind of money without talking to my spouse).

The pressure was a red flag, so I declined to get anything at the time, then spent a few days talking to a few different companies to get their take on it. The consensus was that the repairs he was offering to do were going to be needed eventually - but not immediately - that the solutions he was offering were far more than what we needed - and that even if we had them done, they would cost less than the price we were quoted - even with the discounts.

At the beginning of the appointment, the sweep said that the deal was for an inspection and cleaning - and that if nothing needed to be cleaned we could either apply the difference between what we'd paid and what an inspection typically cost towards any repairs we asked them to make or we'd get refunded. We still haven't been refunded.

Upon reaching out to the owner to inquire, it was suggested that maybe I was supposed to ask Angie's List for the refund. (Angie'sList wasn't all that interested in helping out because we were a few days past the cut-off of their 30-day guarantee... So this is the first and last deal we'll be purchasing from them as well. We've definitely been better served with providers we've found on HomeAdvisor, through personal recommendations, and via conversations we've had on NextDoor.)

So - essentially, we spent $80 to have someone come out and try to convince us to spend $2,500 on repairs to fix a problem that we eventually fixed for $100. We didn't even get a clean fireplace out of the deal (perhaps I was naive in assuming that was part of the cleaning package. If I'd known there would be no refund for not having a cleaning performed, I probably would have made a bigger point about asking about it at the time. Lesson learned.)

The company was prompt, professional, and responsive right up until the appointment. At that time, it felt more like a sales call than an inspection - which is not what we ordered.

I don't blame the poor sweep who showed up. It's not his company and he was just doing his job. I wish I'd at least had a dirty chimney so I could feel like I got something out of the deal. As it was, I spent $80 to learn not to work with this company again.

Update - 11/23
Just received a $30 refund for the cleaning part of the service. Still wouldn't recommend the company based on the sales tactics, but appreciate the refund. Even it if took a while to get.</Text>
